***zege.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zege.html>zege</a> (8297)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēge</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sigi</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*segaz</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeggen</a> (122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seggen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*seggen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sagjaną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sekʷ-</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> irregular <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> tense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:common.html>common</a> Ingvaeonic <a href = vnd.unilang:development.html>development</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:northern.html>northern</a> dialects, seen <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brein.html>brein</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeil.html>zeil</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeggen</a></strong>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intensifier</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> oneself, referring <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:subject.html>subject</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sentence.html>sentence</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:myself.html>myself</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:yourself.html>yourself</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:itself.html>itself</a>, ourselves, themselves <a href = vnd.unilang:etc.html>etc</a>.
